When matched, clears the entire row it is on.\r\n‚úì\tBy matching 4 jewels of the same color in one row, a column buster appears. When matched, clears the entire column it is on.\r\n‚úì\tBy matching 4 jewels of the same color in one column and 3 jewels in one row or vice versa you get a cross buster. When matched, clears the entire row and column it is on.\r\n‚úì\tIf you are able to match 5 jewels, you get a super jewel. This can be switched with any other single jewel on the board. When activated, all the same-colored jewels as the jewel it was switched with, will be removed from the board. If you combine the jewel with a special jewel, all the jewels of that color will change into that special jewel, and activate those special jewels.\r\n‚úì\tBy matching 5 jewels of the same color in one column and 3 jewels in one row or vice versa you get a super cross jewel. This can be switched with any other single jewel on the board. When activated, all the same-colored jewels will transform into cross busters and activate those jewels.\r\n‚úì\tWhen you destroy a line of three you receive 10 points for each jewel in the line.
